Model:     I apologize for the continued errors in the previous plans. I understand that I must strictly adhere to the provided list of valid action instances. It appears I was still trying to generate some `move_base` actions that were not explicitly in the list or was selecting `bconf` and `btraj` values that were not valid for the `place` actions when specific kinematic configurations were required.
           
           Let's re-examine the `move_base` actions very carefully. The valid `move_base` actions are of the form `(move_base ?q1: object, ?q2: object, ?t: object)`. Where `?t` is a `btraj` object. The error messages indicate specific invalid `move_base` actions.
